      "title": "Google Cloud Firestore",
      "url": "https://www.make.com/en/help/apps/database/google-cloud-firestore",
      "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nAirtable\nAmazon Redshift\nBringData.co\nCaspio\nData24-7\nGoogle Cloud Firestore\nKnack\nMySQL\nNinox\nPostgreSQL\nMicrosoft SQL Server\nTadabase\nuProc\nWasabi\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsDatabaseGoogle Cloud Firestore\nGoogle Cloud Firestore\n\nWith Google Cloud Firestore modules in Make, you can work with documents in your Google Cloud Firestore.\n\nTo use the Google Cloud Firestore modules, you must have a Google account and a Firebase project created in your Google Firebase Console. You can create an account at accounts.google.com. See Google's Create a Firebase account documentation for more information regarding how to create a Firebase project.\n\nRefer to the Cloud Firestore API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nNote\n\nMake's use and transfer of information received from Google APIs to any other app will adhere to Google API Services User Data Policy.\n\nConnect Google Cloud Firestore to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Cloud Firestore.\n\nEstablish the connection with Google Cloud Firestore in Make.\n\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Cloud Firestore\n\nBefore you establish the connection in Make, you must create and configure a project in the Google Cloud Console to obtain your client credentials.\n\nCreate a Google Cloud Console project for Google Cloud Firestore\n\nTo create a Google Cloud Console project:\n\nLog in to the Google Cloud Console using your Google credentials.\n\nIn the top menu, click Select a project > New project.\n\nEnter a Project name and select the Location for your project.\n\nClick Create.\n\nIn the top menu, check if your new project is selected in the Select a project dropdown. If not, select the project you just created.\n\nEnable APIs for Google Cloud Firestore\n\nTo enable the required APIs:\n\nOpen the left navigation menu and go to APIs & Services > Library.\n\nSearch for and enable the following APIs: Google Cloud Firestore API, Firebase Management API, and Google Cloud Storage JSON API.\n\nConfigure your OAuth consent screen for Google Cloud Firestore\n\nTo configure your OAuth consent screen:\n\nIn the left sidebar, click OAuth consent screen.\n\nUnder User Type, select External.\n\nFor more information regarding user types, refer to Google's Exceptions to verification requirements documentation.\n\nClick Create.\n\nFill in the required fields with your information.\n\nIn the Authorized domains section, add make.com and integromat.com.\n\nClick Save and continue.\n\nIn the Scopes page, click Add or remove scopes, add the following scopes, and click Update.\n\nhttps://www.googleapis.com/auth/cloud-platform\n\nhttps://www.googleapis.com/auth/datastore\n\nhttps://www.googleapis.com/auth/devstorage.read_write\n\nhttps://www.googleapis.com/auth/firebase.readonly\n\nClick Save and continue.\n\nOptional: If your project will remain in the Testing publishing status, add user emails on the Test users page, then click Save and continue.\n\nCreate your Google Cloud Firestore client credentials\n\nTo create your client credentials:\n\nIn the left sidebar, click Credentials.\n\nClick + Create Credentials > OAuth client ID.\n\nIn the Application type dropdown, select Web application.\n\nUpdate the Name of your OAuth client. This will help you identify it in the console.\n\nIn the Authorized redirect URIs section, click + Add URI and enter the following redirect URI: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/google-custom\n\nClick Create.\n\nCopy your Client ID and Client secret values and store them in a safe place.\n\nYou will use these values in the Client ID and Client Secret fields in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Google Cloud Firestore in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Google Cloud Firestore module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Client ID and Client Secret fields, enter the values you copied in the Create your Google Cloud Firestore client credentials section above.\n\nClick Sign in with Google.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nIf you are connecting to your unverified Google app, you may receive a notice stating Google hasn't verified this app. If so, click Advanced > Go to integromat.com and allow Make (formerly Integromat) access. This allows you to connect to your unverified app.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Google Cloud Firestore modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Google Cloud Firestore Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nDocuments\n\nWatch New Documents\n\nWatch New Documents (Advanced)\n\nCreate a Document\n\nGet a Document\n\nGet Documents\n\nList Documents\n\nList Collection IDs\n\nQuery Documents\n\nNote: Every query requires an index. For the most basic queries, Google Cloud Firestore creates indexes by default. Some queries require you to set up an index manually. Follow the steps below to set up the Index.\n\nRun the Query Documents module with a request that requires creating a new index.\n\nAfter the module fails, open the output, and copy a link under the error message.\n\nOpen the link in your browser. You will be redirected to the Indexes tab in Google Cloud Firestore.\n\nClick Add index.\n\nRun the Query Documents module with the same request again.\n\nUpdate a Document\n\nDelete a Document\n\nStorage\n\nNote: You need to have the Blaze Plan for your Firestore account to use the Storage modules.\n\nBackup to Google Cloud Storage\n\nRestore from Google Cloud Storage\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nGoogle Cloud Firestore\nConnect Google Cloud Firestore to Make\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Cloud Firestore\nEstablish the connection with Google Cloud Firestore in Make\nBuild Google Cloud Firestore Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

      "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\natSpoke\nCanny\nChannels\nCustomerly\nDelighted\nDisqus\nFeedier\nFreshdesk\nFreshservice\nGroove\nHappyFox Help Desk\nHelp Scout\nJitbit\nKiyOh\nLiveAgent\nQualtrics\nReamaze\nRetently\nSatismeter\nServiceNow\nSimplesat\nSolarWinds Service Desk\nSonar\nSupportBee\nSurvicate\nTeamwork Desk\nUserback\nWix Answers\nZammad\nZendesk\nZendesk Guide\nZoho Desk\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCustomer SupportZendesk\nZendesk \n\nWith Zendesk modules in Make you can watch, create, update, list, retrieve, and delete the articles, comments, forum posts, groups, organizations, tickets, and users in your Zendesk account.\n\nTo use the Zendesk modules, you must have a Zendesk account. You can create an account at zendesk.com/register.\n\nRefer to the Zendesk API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Zendesk to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nCreate a custom application in Zendesk to obtain your Unique Identifier and Secret.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nCreate a custom application in Zendesk\n\nTo create a Zendesk custom application and retrieve your client credentials:\n\nLog in to your Zendesk account.\n\nIn the left navigation menu, click Apps and integrations > APIs > Zendesk API.\n\nGo to OAuth Clients and click Add OAuth Clients.\n\nFor Client name, enter a name.\n\nFor Unique identifier, you can use the default suggestion or you can change it. Copy the Unique Identifier value and store it in a safe place.\n\nFor Redirect URLs, enter the following: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/zendesk/\n\nClick Save.\n\nA dialog box will open, advising you that the Secret value will only be shown once. Click OK.\n\nCopy the Secret value and store it in a safe place.\n\nClick Save.\n\nYou will use these values in the Unique Identifier and Secret fields in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Zendesk in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Zendesk module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Domain field, enter your Zendesk domain. You can find your Zendesk domain in your browser's address bar. Example: domain.zendesk.com.\n\nIn the Unique Identifier field, enter the Unique Identifier value copied above.\n\nIn the Secret field, enter the Secret value copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Zendesk modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet up Zendesk Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd a Zendesk instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nSelect the corresponding connection for the webhook in the Connection field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard. You will use this link to set up your webhook in your Zendesk account.\n\nLog in to your Zendesk account.\n\nClick Apps and integrations > Webhooks.\n\nClick Create webhook.\n\nChoose Trigger or automation and click Next.\n\nEnter a name for your webhook.\n\nEnter the Endpoint URL that was copied from Make.\n\nChoose your Request method, Request format, and Authentication type and click Create webhook.\n\nNext, you will need to select a trigger or automation in the Admin Center. Click Add trigger and enter a name.\n\nChoose a Category.\n\nSet the conditions that are necessary for the trigger to run.\n\nUnder Actions, select Notify by > active webhook and then choose your new webhook that you just created. Click Create.\n\nReturn to the Webhooks page and click Finish setup.\n\nZendesk will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nTriggers\nWatch Tickets\nWatch Tickets in a View\nWatch Ticket Activity\nList Tickets\nSearch Tickets\nList Soft Deleted Tickets\nGet a Ticket\nCreates a Ticket\nUpdate a Ticket\nMerge Tickets\nSoft Delete a Ticket\nPermanently Deletes a CenterAppsDatabaseAirtable\nAirtable \n\nThe Airtable modules allow you to monitor records and submitted forms or search, retrieve, create, update, and delete records in your Airtable account.\n\nTo get started with Airtable, create an account at airtable.com/signup.\n\nRefer to the Airtable REST API Documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Airtable to Make\n\nYou can connect Airtable apps in Make in three ways:\n\nConnect using OAuth\n\nConnect using Personal Access Token\n\nConnect using API Key (deprecated January 2024)\n\nConnect using OAuth\n\nTo connect Airtable using OAuth:\n\nLog in to your Make account, open the Airtable module scenario, click the Add button next to the Connection type field, and select Airtable OAuth.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show Advanced Settings and enter the client credentials created in the section, Obtain OAuth Credentials.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIn the Credentials\nConnect using Personal Access Token\n\nYou can connect Airtable apps using personal access token values from your Airtable account.\n\nLog in to your Airtable account.\n\nClick Your Profile Icon > Developer hub.\n\nClick Personal access tokens > Create new token.\n\nEnter a name for the access token, select the Scopes, Access, and click Create token.\n\nNote: Users should choose at least the following most frequently required scopes: data.records:read, data.records:write, and schema.bases:read\n\nCopy the Personal Access Token to a safe place, and click Done.\n\nLog in to your Make account, open the Airtable module scenario, click the Add button next to the Connection type field, and select the connection type as Airtable Token or Key.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nSelect the token type as Personal Access Token and enter the token copied in step 5 above.\n\nOptional: Click Show Advanced Settingsand select the proxy service in the Proxy field.\n\nNote\n\nBy choosing a Proxy, you understand and confirm that your Airtable data, including personal access tokens, will be routed through a third-party service.\n\nClick Save.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Airtable modules. You can create an account at caspio.com.\n\nRefer to the Caspio API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Caspio to Make\n\nTo connect Caspio to Make, you must first obtain the Client ID, and Client Secret values from your Caspio account.\n\nTo establish the connection:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Caspio module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the  Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Subdomain field, enter your Subdomain. You can create an account at www.zoho.com/desk.\n\nRefer to the Zoho Desk API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Zoho Desk to Make\n\nTo connect your Zoho Desk account to Make you must first obtain your Organization ID.\n\nTo establish the connection:\n\nLog in to your Zoho Desk account.\n\nClick on the Setup icon in the top-right corner to open the Setup page.\n\nIn the Developer Space section, click on API.\n\nIn the Zoho Service Communication (ZSC) Key section, copy the OrgId value. You will use this value in the Organization ID field in Make.\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Zoho Desk module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Organization ID field, enter the OrgID value copied in step 4.\n\nIn the Domain Extension field, select the domain that corresponds to your account location.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom app client credentials. For more information, refer to the Zoho Desk Authentication (OAuth) page.\n\nIf requested, use the following Redirect URI when creating your custom app: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/zoho-desk.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Zoho Desk modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Zoho Desk Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nActions\n\nGet an Object\n\nCreate an Object\n\nDelete an Object\n\nUpdate an Object\n\nAdd a Comment\n\nClose Tickets\n\nEdit Spam Objects\n\nMake an API Call\n\nSearches\n\nSearch Objects\n\nList Objects\n\nZoho Desk\nConnect Zoho Desk to Make\nBuild Zoho Desk Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you don't have an AWS account, you can create it here: https://aws.amazon.com/console. If you don't have a running cluster, you can look at the guides provided by Amazon, here: http://docs.aws.amazon.com/redshift/latest/gsg/rs-gsg-launch-sample-cluster.html.\n\nDon't forget to enable access for your cluster from the Internet so, Make can actually receive access.\n\nConnecting Amazon Redshift to Make\n\nTo connect your Amazon Redshift cluster to Make, follow the general instructions for Connecting to services.\n\nYou will be prompted to enter the following:\n\nhost: your cluster URL, which you get in your AWS Console\n\nport: port on which your database is running, default is 5439\n\nuser\n\npassword\n\ndatabase\n\nAfter you have filled all required fields you can click 'Continue'. Make will try to establish a connection to your database. If it succeeds, the dialog will close and you will be able to continue setting up your module.\n\nMake will make connections to your database from specific IP addresses. Our servers are set up with valid PTR records so you can easily restrict access by allowing %.make.com.\n\nAmazon Redshift\nGetting started with Amazon Web Services Redshift\nConnecting Amazon Redshift to Make\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

      "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\natSpoke\nCanny\nChannels\nCustomerly\nDelighted\nDisqus\nFeedier\nFreshdesk\nFreshservice\nGroove\nHappyFox Help Desk\nHelp Scout\nJitbit\nKiyOh\nLiveAgent\nQualtrics\nReamaze\nRetently\nSatismeter\nServiceNow\nSimplesat\nSolarWinds Service Desk\nSonar\nSupportBee\nSurvicate\nTeamwork Desk\nUserback\nWix Answers\nZammad\nZendesk\nZendesk Guide\nZoho Desk\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCustomer SupportTeamwork Desk\nTeamwork Desk\n\nWith Teamwork Desk modules in Make, you can mange the tickets, customer data, helpdocs sites, categories, and articles in your Teamwork Desk account.\n\nTo use Teamwork Desk modules, you must have a Teamwork Desk account. You can create an account at teamwork.com/desk-signup.\n\nRefer to the Teamwork Desk API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Teamwork Desk to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Teamwork Desk.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Teamwork Desk\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Teamwork Desk account:\n\nLog in to your Teamwork Desk account.\n\nClick the profile icon in the bottom-left corner.\n\nClick View Profile > API Keys.\n\nClick Create an API Key and select the V1 API Key option.\n\nCopy the API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Teamwork Desk in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Teamwork Desk module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nChoose your Site Address.\n\nIf you chose Teamwork site address in the field above, enter Your Teamwork domain. For example, Your_Domain.teamwork.com.\n\nIf you chose Custom domain in the field above, enter Your Custom Domain. For example, projects.mysite.com.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Teamwork Desk modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet up Teamwork Desk Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd a Teamwork Desk instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nSelect the corresponding connection for the webhook in the Connection field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nLog in to your Teamwork Desk account.\n\nClick the profile icon in the bottom-left corner.\n\nClick Settings > Webhooks.\n\nClick Add webhook.\n\nIn the Payload URL field, enter the webhook copied in step 4 above.\n\nIn the Content Type field, select the option from the drop-down list appropriately.\n\nIn the Token field, enter a unique custom password and click Save.\n\nTeamwork Desk will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nNote\n\nAt the time of this publication, all steps for Obtain your Teamwork Desk API and Set up Teamwork Desk Webhooks were checked and verified to be accurate. However this may have changed, so please see the Teamwork Desk documentation for the most up-to-date directions.\n\nBuild Teamwork Desk Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nEvent\n\nWatch Events\n\nTicket\n\nList Tickets\n\nGet Ticket\n\nCreate Ticket\n\nThis module relies on the V1 Teamwork Desk API. CenterAppsCustomer SupportSimplesat\nSimplesat\n\nWith the Simplesat modules in Make you can:\n\ncreate or update a customer\n\nwatch and list answers\n\nTo get started with Simplesat, create an account at Simplesat.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnect Simplesat to Make\n\nTo connect your Simplesat account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Simplesat account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your Simplesat account.\n\nClick Admin > Account Settings.\n\nCopy the Account Key to the clipboard.\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a module from the Simplesat app into an Make scenario.\n\nClick Add next to the Connection field.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the details copied in step 3 and click Continue.\n\nYou have successfully connected Simplesat app with Make and can now create scenarios.\n\nCustomer\n\nYou can create or update the customers.\n\nCreate or Update Customer\n\nCreates a new or updates an existing customer.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Simplesat account.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the customer's email address.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the customer's name.\n\n\n\n\nCompany Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the customer's company name.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Attributes\n\n\t\n\nYou can include multiple custom attributes with each customer record to use as rules for your audience. For example, person type, company status, and user role.\n\nSimplesat checks whether the custom attribute exists:\n\nIf the specified custom attribute exists, the record will be updated,\n\nIf the specified customer attribute does not exist, a new custom attribute will be created.\n\nItem\n\n\t\n\nEnter the customer attributes details.\n\nKey\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the attribute name. For example, company.\n\n\n\n\nValue\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the attribute value. For example, company name.\n\nAnswer\n\nYou can create and run the following answer modules.\n\nWatch Answers\n\nTriggers when an answer is created and updated.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Simplesat account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of answers Make will return during one execution cycle. The default value is 2.\n\nList Answers\n\nReturns a list of all answers.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Simplesat account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of answers Make will return during one execution cycle. The default value is 2.\n\nOther\n\nYou can call APIs using the Make an API Call module.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Simplesat account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.simplesat.io/api. For example: /answers.\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Simplesat API Documentation..\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET\n\nto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST\n\nto create a new entry.\n\nPUT\n\nto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH\n\nto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE\n\nto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't need to add authorization headers; we've already added those for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Posts\n\nThe following API call creates or updates the customer in your Simplesat account:\n\nURL:\n\n/customers/create-or-update/\n\nMethod:\n\nPOST\n\nHeaders:\n\nKey: X-Simplesat-Token\n\nValue: {{your access token}}\n\nThe result can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body. \n\nIn our example, a new customer is created with the specified details:\n\nSimplesat\nConnect Simplesat to Make\nCustomer\nCreate or Update Customer\nAnswer\nWatch Answers\nList Answers\nOther\nMake an API Call\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

      "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\natSpoke\nCanny\nChannels\nCustomerly\nDelighted\nDisqus\nFeedier\nFreshdesk\nFreshservice\nGroove\nHappyFox Help Desk\nHelp Scout\nJitbit\nKiyOh\nLiveAgent\nQualtrics\nReamaze\nRetently\nSatismeter\nServiceNow\nSimplesat\nSolarWinds Service Desk\nSonar\nSupportBee\nSurvicate\nTeamwork Desk\nUserback\nWix Answers\nZammad\nZendesk\nZendesk Guide\nZoho Desk\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCustomer SupportFreshdesk\nFreshdesk\n\nWith Freshdesk modules in Make, you can manage the events, tickets, conversations, contacts, companies, forums, and agents in your Freshdesk account.\n\nTo use the Freshdesk modules, you must have a Freshdesk account. You can create an account at freshdesk.com.\n\nRefer to the Freshdesk API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Freshdesk to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Freshdesk.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Freshdesk\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Freshdesk account:\n\nLog in to your Freshdesk account.\n\nIn the upper-right corner, click on your profile picture and select Profile Settings.\n\nIn the right sidebar, click the View API key button.\n\nCopy the API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API key field in Make.\n\nNote\n\nAt the time of this publication, all steps for Obtain your API key in Freshdesk were checked and verified to be accurate. However this may have changed, so please see the Freshdesk Support documentation for the most up-to-date directions.\n\nEstablish the connection with Freshdesk in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Frsehdesk module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nIn the Company name field, enter your domain name. If your Freshdesk URL is https://abc.freshdesk.com then enter abc here.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Freshdesk modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet up Freshdesk Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd an Freshdesk instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nSelect the corresponding connection for the webhook in the Connection field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nLog in to your Freshdesk account.\n\nFollow the directions as outlined in the Freshdesk Using Webhooks in Automation documentation.\n\nFreshdesk will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nBuild Freshdesk Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nEvent\n\nWatch Events\n\nTicket\n\nWatch Tickets\n\nSearch Tickets by Query\n\nSearch/List Tickets\n\nList Ticket Conversations\n\nList Time Entries\n\nList Satisfaction Ratings\n\nGet a Ticket\n\nCreate a Ticket\n\nCreate an Outbound Email\n\nUpdate a Ticket\n\nDelete a Ticket\n\nConversation\n\nCreate a Reply\n\nCreate a Note\n\nContact\n\nWatch Contacts\n\nSearch Contacts\n\nSearch/List Contacts\n\nGet a Contact\n\nCreate a Contact\n\nUpdate a Contact\n\nDelete a Contact\n\nCompany\n\nSearch Companies\n\nGet a Company\n\nCreate a Company\n\nUpdate a Company\n\nDelete a Company\n\nForum\n\nCreate a Forum\n\nCreate a Forum Category\n\nCreate a Forum Topic\n\nOther\n\nGet an Agent\n\nMake an API Call\n\nFreshdesk\nConnect Freshdesk to Make\nObtain your API key in Freshdesk\nEstablish the connection with Freshdesk in Make\nSet up Freshdesk Webhooks\nBuild Freshdesk Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create an atSpoke account at atspoke.com.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnect atSpoke to Make\n\nTo connect your atSpoke account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your atSpoke account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\n1. Log in to your atSpoke account.\n\n2. Click Your Account > My Profile > API.\n\n3. Go to Make and open the atSpoke module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n4. Copy the API Key to your clipboard.\n\n5. Go to Make and open the atSpoke module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n6. In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\n7. In the API Key field, enter the API key copied in step 4, and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nResources\nWatch New Resources\n\nTriggers when a new resource is created.\n\nNote\n\nYou do not have to add the webhooks in the atSpoke as it is automatically done for you once you add and save an instant trigger module to your scenario.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your atSpoke account.\n\n\n\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter the details about the trigger.\n\nList Resources\n\nReturns a list of resources.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your atSpoke account.\n\n\n\n\nSearch Query\n\n\t\n\nEnter the keyword or phrase to list the resources based on the specified query.\n\n\n\n\nAI\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to use AI to list the resources.\n\n\n\n\nStatus\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status of the resource you want to list:\n\nOK\n\nNeeds Review\n\nDeprecated\n\n\n\n\nTeam\n\n\t\n\nSelect the team whose resources you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nAuthor\n\n\t\n\nSelect the authors whose resources you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nReview By\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date to list the resources that should be reviewed by the specified date. number.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user's email address.\n\n\n\n\nUnique ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user's unique ID for identification.\n\n\n\n\nJob Title\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user's job position. For example, Product Manager.\n\n\n\n\nLocation\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user's work or home address.\n\n\n\n\nDepartment\n\n\t\n\nEnter the department in which the user works. For example, Engineering.\n\n\n\n\nManager\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user's manager name.\n\n\n\n\nStart Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user's job start date. See the list of supported date and time formats.\n\nOther\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your atSpoke account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.askspoke.com/api. For example: /v1/users\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the atSpoke API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET to retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST to create a new entry.\n\nPUT to update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH to make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE to delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Users\n\nThe following API call returns all the users from your atSpoke account:\n\nURL: /v1/users\n\nMethod: GET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > results In our example, 3 users were returned:\n\natSpoke\nGetting Started with atSpoke\nConnect atSpoke to Make\nResources\nWatch New Resources\nList Resources\nGet a Resource\nCreate a Resource\nUpdate a Resource\nDelete a Resource\nRequests\nWatch New Requests\nWatch Requests Updated\nList Requests\nGet a Request\nCreate a Request\nUpdate a Request\nDelete a Request\nUsers\nList Users\nGet a User\nUpdate a User\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Users\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an account at zoho.com/in/inventory.\n\nRefer to the Zoho Inventory API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Zoho Inventory to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your Organization ID in Zoho Inventory.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your Organization ID in Zoho Inventory\n\nTo obtain your Organization ID from your Zoho Inventory account:\n\nLog in to your Zoho Inventory account.\n\nIn the upper-right corner, click your profile icon.\n\nYour Organization ID is shown at the top of the menu.\n\nCopy the Organization ID value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the Organization ID field in Make.\n\nNote\n\nAt the time of this publication, all steps for Obtain your Organization ID in Zoho Inventory were checked and verified to be accurate. However this may have changed, so please see the Zoho Inventory Help Docs for the most up-to-date directions.\n\nEstablish the connection with Zoho Inventory in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Zoho Inventory module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nIn the Connection type field, choose Zoho Inventory OAuth2.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Region field, choose your region. For example, if the URL of your account is e.g. https://inventory.zoho.eu, then select the EU option.\n\nIn the Organization field, enter the Organization ID copied above.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom app client credentials. For more information, refer to the Zoho Inventory Help Docs regarding custom connections.\n\nIf requested, use the following Redirect URI when creating your custom app: https://www.make.com/oauth/cb/zoho-inventory2.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Zoho Inventory modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Zoho Inventory Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nContacts\n\nWatch Contacts\n\nSearch Contacts\n\nGet a Contact\n\nCreate a Contact\n\nUpdate a Contact\n\nDelete a Contact\n\nMark a Contact Active/Inactive\n\nContact Person\n\nList Contact Persons\n\nGet a Contact Person\n\nCreate a Contact Person\n\nUpdate a Contact Person\n\nDelete a Contact Person\n\nMark a Contact Person Primary\n\nItem Groups\n\nWatch Item Groups\n\nList Item Groups\n\nGet an Item Group\n\nCreate an Item Group\n\nUpdate an Item Group\n\nDelete an Item Group\n\nItems\n\nWatch Items\n\nList Items\n\nGet an Item\n\nCreate an Item\n\nUpdate an Item\n\nItem Adjustments\n\nWatch Item Adjustments\n\nList Item Adjustments\n\nGet an Item Adjustment\n\nCreate an Item Adjustment\n\nDelete an Item Adjustment\n\nMark an Item Active/Inactive\n\nSales Order\n\nWatch Sales Orders\n\nList Sales Orders\n\nGet a Sales Order\n\nCreate a Sales Order\n\nUpdate a Sales Order\n\nDelete a Sales Order\n\nPackages\n\nWatch Packages\n\nSearch Packages\n\nGet a Package\n\nCreate a Package\n\nUpdate a Package\n\nDelete a Package\n\nShipment Orders\n\nGet a Shipment Order\n\nCreate a Shipment Order\n\nMark a Shipment Order as Delivered\n\nDelete a Shipment Order\n\nPurchase Orders\n\nWatch Purchase Orders\n\nList Purchase Orders\n\nGet a Purchase Order\n\nCreate a Purchase Order\n\nUpdate a Purchase Order\n\nDelete a Purchase Order\n\nInvoices\n\nWatch Invoices\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nZoho Inventory\nConnect Zoho Inventory to Make\nObtain your Organization ID in Zoho Inventory\nEstablish the connection with Zoho Inventory in Make\nBuild Zoho Inventory Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an account at zoho.com.\n\nRefer to the Zoho CRM API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Zoho CRM to Make\nWarning\n\nIf you have more then one connection created to your Zoho CRM account, the Zoho CRM modules will not work.\n\nTo establish the connection:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Zoho CRM module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Domain field, select the applicable domain for your account.\n\nOptional: Click Show Advanced Settings and enter your custom app client credentials or manually add scopes. You must have a Zoho developer account to create custom apps. For more information, refer to the Zoho CRM Register your Application guide.\n\nIf requested, use the following Redirect URI when creating your custom app: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/zohocrm2.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Zoho CRM modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Zoho CRM Scenarios\nModules\nList Modules\nFields\nList Fields\nUsers\nAdd Users\nSearch Users\nDelete a User\nObjects\nWatch Objects\nCreate an Object\nDelete an Object\nGet an Object\nUpdate an Object\nList Objects\nSearch Objects\nLeads\nUpsert a Lead\nRelated Records\nUpdate a Related Record\nList Related Record\nDelete a Related Record\nTags\nAdd a Tag to a Record\nRemove a Tag from a Record\nCreate a Tag\nUpdate a Tag\nSearch Tags\nDelete a Tag\nAttachments\nPhotos\nUpload a Photo\nMake an API Call\nStep by step guide to call APIs\nTroubleshooting\nHow To Remove the Make App Token from your Zoho Account\nError AUTHENTICATION_FAILURE\nZoho CRM\nConnect Zoho CRM to Make\nBuild Zoho CRM Scenarios\nModules\nFields\nUsers\nObjects\nLeads\nRelated Records\nTags\nAttachments\nPhotos\nMake an API Call\nTroubleshooting\nHow To Remove the Make App Token from your Zoho Account\nError AUTHENTICATION_FAILURE\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."
